<td align="center" colspan="5" style="background:#BFD7FF; border-top:1px solid #aaa; border-bottom:1px solid #aaa;"><b><a href="/wiki/%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8" title="올림픽 오스트레일리아 선수단">올림픽 오스트레일리아 선수단</a></b></td>

<p><b><a href="/wiki/%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8" title="올림픽 오스트레일리아 선수단">오스트레일리아</a></b>는 <a href="/wiki/2000%EB%85%84" title="2000년">2000년</a> 8월 13일부터 29일까지 자국 <a href="/wiki/%EC%8B%9C%EB%93%9C%EB%8B%88" title="시드니">시드니</a>에서 열린 <b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%EC%A0%9C28%ED%9A%8C_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD" title="제28회 하계 올림픽">제28회 하계 올림픽</a></b>에 참가했다.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id=".EC.A2.85.EB.AA.A9.EB.B3.84_.EC.84.B1.EC.A0.81">종목별 성적</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="부분 편집: 종목별 성적">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id=".EB.B0.B0.EA.B5.AC"><a class="image" href="/wiki/%ED%8C%8C%EC%9D%BC:Basketball_pictogram.svg"><img alt="Basketball pictogram.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" height="30" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Basketball_pictogram.svg/30px-Basketball_pictogram.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Basketball_pictogram.svg/45px-Basketball_pictogram.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Basketball_pictogram.svg/60px-Basketball_pictogram.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a> 배구</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="부분 편집: 배구">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<hr/>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EB%B0%B0%EA%B5%AC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="2000년 하계 올림픽 배구 (없는 문서)">2000년 하계 올림픽 배구</a>입니다.</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id=".EB.82.A8.EC.9E.90">남자</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="부분 편집: 남자">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul>
<li><b>Preliminary Round</b>
<ul>
<li>Lost to Canada (90-101)</li>
<li>Lost to Yugoslavia (66-80)</li>
<li>Defeated Russia (75-71)</li>
<li>Defeated Angola (86-75)</li>
<li>Defeated Spain (91-80)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Quarterfinals</b>
<ul>
<li>Defeated Italy (65-62)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Semi-finals</b>
<ul>
<li>Lost to France (52-76)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Bronze Medal Match</b>
<ul>
<li>Lost to Lithuania (71-89)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id=".EC.97.AC.EC.9E.90">여자</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="부분 편집: 여자">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul>
<li><b>Preliminary Round</b>
<ul>
<li>Defeated Canada (76-48)</li>
<li>Defeated Brazil (81-70)</li>
<li>Defeated Slovakia (70-47)</li>
<li>Defeated Senegal (96-39)</li>
<li>Defeated France (69-62)</li>
</ul>

<li><b>Quarterfinals</b>
<ul>
<li>Defeated Poland (76-48)</li>
</ul>

</ul>
</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id=".EB.B0.B0.EB.93.9C.EB.AF.BC.ED.84.B4"><a class="image" href="/wiki/%ED%8C%8C%EC%9D%BC:Badminton_pictogram.svg"><img alt="Badminton pictogram.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" height="30" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Badminton_pictogram.svg/30px-Badminton_pictogram.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Badminton_pictogram.svg/45px-Badminton_pictogram.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Badminton_pictogram.svg/60px-Badminton_pictogram.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a> 배드민턴</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="부분 편집: 배드민턴">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<hr/>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EB%B0%B0%EB%93%9C%EB%AF%BC%ED%84%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="2000년 하계 올림픽 배드민턴 (없는 문서)">2000년 하계 올림픽 배드민턴</a>입니다.</div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id=".EC.95.BC.EA.B5.AC"><a class="image" href="/wiki/%ED%8C%8C%EC%9D%BC:Baseball_pictogram.svg"><img alt="Baseball pictogram.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" height="30" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Baseball_pictogram.svg/30px-Baseball_pictogram.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Baseball_pictogram.svg/45px-Baseball_pictogram.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Baseball_pictogram.svg/60px-Baseball_pictogram.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a> 야구</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="부분 편집: 야구">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<hr/>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a href="/wiki/2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%95%BC%EA%B5%AC" title="2000년 하계 올림픽 야구">2000년 하계 올림픽 야구</a>입니다.</div>
<p><br/>
The Australians' second appearance in the Olympic baseball tournament resulted in the team moving up one place in the rankings, from seventh to sixth. They defeated <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Korea_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Korea at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Korea</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=South_Africa_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="South Africa at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">South Africa</a> but lost to the five other teams in competition to finish outside the top four and find themselves eliminated after the preliminaries.</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Preliminary Round Robin</b>
<ul>
<li>Lost to Netherlands (4-6)</li>
<li>Defeated Korea (5-3)</li>
<li>Lost to Japan (3-7)</li>
<li>Defeated South Africa (10-4)</li>
<li>Lost to Cuba (0-1)</li>
<li>Lost to Italy (7-8)</li>
<li>Lost to United States (1-12) → did not advance</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Canoeing">Canoeing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="부분 편집: Canoeing">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Canoeing_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Canoeing at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Canoeing at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id=".EC.88.98.EC.83.81_.EA.B2.BD.EA.B8.B0"><a class="image" href="/wiki/%ED%8C%8C%EC%9D%BC:Swimming_pictogram.svg"><img alt="Swimming pictogram.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" height="30" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Swimming_pictogram.svg/30px-Swimming_pictogram.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Swimming_pictogram.svg/45px-Swimming_pictogram.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Swimming_pictogram.svg/60px-Swimming_pictogram.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a> 수상 경기</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="부분 편집: 수상 경기">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<hr/>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id=".EB.8B.A4.EC.9D.B4.EB.B9.99"><a class="image" href="/wiki/%ED%8C%8C%EC%9D%BC:Diving_pictogram.svg"><img alt="Diving pictogram.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" height="30" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Diving_pictogram.svg/30px-Diving_pictogram.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Diving_pictogram.svg/45px-Diving_pictogram.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Diving_pictogram.svg/60px-Diving_pictogram.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a> 다이빙</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="부분 편집: 다이빙">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a href="/wiki/2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EB%8B%A4%EC%9D%B4%EB%B9%99" title="2000년 하계 올림픽 다이빙">2000년 하계 올림픽 다이빙</a>입니다.</div>
<p>Australia entered divers in all of the events, and won two bronze medals. <b>남자</b></p>

<p><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%ED%8B%80:Infobox_Olympics_Australia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="틀:Infobox Olympics Australia (없는 문서)">틀:Infobox Olympics Australia</a></p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id=".EC.88.98.EC.98.81"><a class="image" href="/wiki/%ED%8C%8C%EC%9D%BC:Swimming_pictogram.svg"><img alt="Swimming pictogram.svg" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="300" height="30" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Swimming_pictogram.svg/30px-Swimming_pictogram.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Swimming_pictogram.svg/45px-Swimming_pictogram.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Swimming_pictogram.svg/60px-Swimming_pictogram.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a> 수영</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="부분 편집: 수영">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<hr/>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a href="/wiki/2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%88%98%EC%98%81" title="2000년 하계 올림픽 수영">2000년 하계 올림픽 수영</a>입니다.</div>
<p>Australia was very successful in the swimming venue at the 2000 Olympics. They won 5 Gold, 9 Silver, and 4 Bronze medals. The biggest rivalry, both in the press and in the pool, was between the United States and Australia relay teams. In the 4 x 100 m relay, the Americans had won the event every time it had been contested. Australia was able to edge out the Americans by .19 seconds to win the gold medal. The Australians also set three world records. The 2000 Olympics also saw the emergence of <a href="/wiki/%EC%9D%B4%EC%96%B8_%EC%86%8C%ED%94%84" title="이언 소프">이언 소프</a> as an Olympic champion in the Men's 400 m Freestyle.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Equestrianism">Equestrianism</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="부분 편집: Equestrianism">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Equestrianism_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Equestrianism at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Equestrianism at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fencing">Fencing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="부분 편집: Fencing">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Fencing_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Fencing at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Fencing at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>
<p>Seven fencers, five men and two women, represented Australia in 2000.</p>
<dl>
<dt><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Fencing_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_foil&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Fencing at the 2000 Summer Olympics – Men's foil (없는 문서)">Men's foil</a></dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Gerald_McMahon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Gerald McMahon (없는 문서)">Gerald McMahon</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Fencing_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_%C3%A9p%C3%A9e&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Fencing at the 2000 Summer Olympics – Men's épée (없는 문서)">Men's épée</a></dt>
</dl>

<li><b>Preliminary Round (Group B)</b>
<ul>
<li>Australia — Poland 4-0</li>
<li>Australia — India 2-2</li>
<li>Australia — Spain 2-2</li>
<li>Australia — Argentina 2-1</li>
<li>Australia — South Korea 2-1</li>
</ul>

</ul>

</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rhythmic_gymnastics">Rhythmic gymnastics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="부분 편집: Rhythmic gymnastics">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rhythmic_gymnastics_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rhythmic gymnastics at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Rhythmic gymnastics at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sailing">Sailing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="부분 편집: Sailing">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Sailing_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Sailing at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Sailing at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>
<p>Australia competed in all of the sailing events at the 2000 Olympics. They won 2 golds, 1 silver and 1 bronze.</p>

<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Softball_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Softball at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Softball at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Synchronized_swimming">Synchronized swimming</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="부분 편집: Synchronized swimming">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Wrestling">Wrestling</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2000%EB%85%84_%ED%95%98%EA%B3%84_%EC%98%AC%EB%A6%BC%ED%94%BD_%EC%98%A4%EC%8A%A4%ED%8A%B8%EB%A0%88%EC%9D%BC%EB%A6%AC%EC%95%84_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="부분 편집: Wrestling">원본 편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="rellink relarticle mainarticle"><img alt="" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/16px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/24px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg/32px-Crystal_Clear_app_xmag.svg.png 2x" width="16"/> 이 부분의 본문은 <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Wrestling_at_the_2000_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Wrestling at the 2000 Summer Olympics (없는 문서)">Wrestling at the 2000 Summer Olympics</a>입니다.</div>
